<text>I've been enjoying take out from China Station for the last 25 years and I've yet to find anything that compares! I grew up about 5 minutes from the restaurant, but kept going as we moved across town. Nothing else is as good! I've since moved out of the area, but it is the first place I think of eating at every time I come back into town. The hot and spicy chicken with garlic sauce, chicken chow mein, and sweet and sour pork are my favorites. Oh, and the wantons! They're amazing! China Station is the first take out I ordered when quarantine started to ease up. Ordering ahead of time has never worked for us - we have to order in-person and wait while they make the food - but I just accept that and know it's worth the wait every time! I just ate there and I'm already craving more!< /text>< UserId.>
